Obligation:
Clauses:

test_fun(I, J) :- loop(I, J, 0).
loop(I, J, C) :- ','(>=(I, 0), ','(is(J1, 0), inner_loop(I, J1, C))).
loop(I, J, C) :- <(I, 0).
inner_loop(I, J, C) :- ','(=<(J, -(I, 1)), ','(is(J1, +(J, 1)), ','(is(C1, +(C, 1)), inner_loop(I, J1, C1)))).
inner_loop(I, J, C) :- ','(>(J, -(I, 1)), ','(is(I1, -(I, 1)), loop(I1, J, C))).
